<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column1879_c86eeb-98 inner-column-1"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id1879_83ddb0-bc alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column1879_9051c9-b9"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h1 class="kt-adv-heading1879_c509f2-3c wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading1879_c509f2-3c">She Roams The Globe</h1>
</div></div>

</div></div>


<p class="has-text-align-center">Hi everyone! I’m Charlie, the voice behind She Roams The Globe!</p>



<p class="has-text-align-center">I&#8217;ve spent the last 10 years exploring the world and have visited over 40 countries during this time. From <strong><a href="https://sheroamstheglobe.com/iceland/">Iceland</a></strong> to <strong><a href="https://sheroamstheglobe.com/new-zealand/">New Zealand</a></strong>, and plenty of <a href="https://sheroamstheglobe.com/destinations/"><strong>places in between</strong></a>, I share my travel experiences so you can get the most out of your trip. </p>



<p class="has-text-align-center">Whether it&#8217;s climbing volcanoes in <strong><a href="https://sheroamstheglobe.com/guatemala/">Guatemala</a></strong> or getting scammed in <strong><a href="https://sheroamstheglobe.com/indonesia/">Bali</a></strong> (don&#8217;t worry, I&#8217;ve made the mistakes so you don&#8217;t have to!), I’ve got plenty of wild stories and useful tips to share with you.</p>



<p class="has-text-align-center" style="padding-right:var(--wp--preset--spacing--30);padding-left:var(--wp--preset--spacing--30)">If you&#8217;re on the hunt for the best vegan food around the globe, planning an epic road trip or looking for detailed itineraries and guides, I&#8217;m here to help you plan your next adventure!</p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-advancedbtn kb-buttons-wrap kb-btns1879_99a8aa-dd"><a class="kb-button kt-button button kb-btn1879_26ca1c-0d kt-btn-size-standard kt-btn-width-type-auto kb-btn-global-inherit  kt-btn-has-text-true kt-btn-has-svg-false  wp-block-button__link wp-block-kadence-singlebtn" href="https://sheroamstheglobe.com/she-roams-the-globe-about-me/"><span class="kt-btn-inner-text">Learn More About Me Here!</span></a></div>
</div></div>

</div></div>

<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id1879_b97aea-94 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column1879_fdd1a3-76"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h6 class="kt-adv-heading1879_b83a41-e1 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading1879_b83a41-e1">Where are you going?</h6>



<h2 class="kt-adv-heading1879_3890c0-ad wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading1879_3890c0-ad">Travel By Destination</h2>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id1879_52ce91-52 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-5-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-middle">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column1879_5469ca-e0 kb-section-has-link"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">

<h3 class="kt-adv-heading1879_465b19-cf wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading1879_465b19-cf">Indonesia</h3>

<h3 class="kt-adv-heading1879_8058ba-1b wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading1879_8058ba-1b">New Zealand</h3>

<h6 class="kt-adv-heading1879_cf8ba3-b3 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading1879_cf8ba3-b3">Explore</h6>



<h2 class="kt-adv-heading1879_f87e21-a0 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading1879_f87e21-a0">Iceland</h2>



<p>Iceland is easily one of the most unreal places I’ve ever been — I’ve been twice now, and I’d go back in a heartbeat (with a few more layers next time, because summer in Iceland definitely doesn’t mean warm).</p>



<p>My first trip was a nine-day campervan loop around the Ring Road in July, where we chased waterfalls, hiked lava fields, and ate dinner at midnight because the sun just didn’t set. </p>



<p>I still haven’t seen the northern lights in winter, but that just means I’ve got to go back.</p>



<p>Volcanoes, glaciers, black sand beaches, steamy hot springs &#8211; Iceland is wild, quirky, and completely magical.</p>



<p><strong>My top Iceland recommendations:</strong></p>
